We do this in order for the selected currency to remain selected and consistent when browsing our website so that the prices can convert to your (the visitor) local currency.<br/><br/>You are free to refuse our request for your personal information, with the understanding that we may be unable to provide you with some of your desired services.<br/><br/>Your continued use of our website will be regarded as acceptance of our practices around privacy and personal information.
